Major Fires Occur in Guangzhou for Several Days, 17 Shops Destroyed on Baqi Road, Eastern Bund, 47 Businesses Burned Down in Henan 40

Guangzhou Correspondence: In Guangzhou City, in recent days, due to the dryness of late autumn and arid weather, and the occasional carelessness of citizens who do not guard against fire, disasters have been reported frequently. After the great fire at Xin Shengsha in Dongguan, which burned down hundreds of shops, two more major fires have occurred continuously in the southeast of the city in the last two days. Each incident has resulted in the destruction of dozens of shops, causing significant losses and constituting a great calamity for the citizens. The situation of the fires on the Eastern Bund and in Henan in recent days is summarized below:

Eastern Bund

Although the roads on the Eastern Bund of Guangzhou City have been widened recently, the shops are still densely packed. Among them, Qichang Store, No. 22 Baqi Main Road, has been engaged in the electric oil business, supplying automobiles coming and going. Usually, dozens of boxes of electric oil are stored in the store. At about 2:00 PM on the afternoon of the 13th, a partner accidentally left embers, which ignited the wooden planks of the room. Immediately, flames burst forth. By the time they ran out to sound the whistle and call the police, the flames had already spread to the electric oil stored in the store. At this point, it became an uncontrollable fire. Although the fire brigade made every effort to extinguish it, in an instant, it spread to the nearby Baqi Second Road. Refugees in the fire field, supporting the old and carrying the young, risked escaping from the thick smoke. Five or six people fell and were injured along the way. Fortunately, the incident occurred during the daytime, making rescue relatively easier. However, the fire burned until 5:00 PM before it was extinguished. A total of 19 shops were burned down. Those burned down on Baqi Main Road include: Tongfuhao, the Regimental Headquarters of the 914th Regiment of the 152nd Division, Yadong Steel Factory, Qichang Electric Oil Store, Yongguang Electric Oil Store, Feilun Rickshaw Factory, Heli Electric Oil Store, Taixinglong Freight Yard, Faxing Coal Factory, and Faxing Warehouse. Those burned down on Baqi Second Road include: Xinhe Firewood Store, Shengchang Store, Sihe Store, Hongsheng Store, Xiangjihao, and Liuxingjihao, as well as one empty shop. A small boat near the bank was also destroyed by the fire.

Henan

The Buliu Bank of Henan in Guangzhou has a vast area and dense population. The Xishi Main Street is located there, with no roads yet closed, and shops face each other, only a short distance apart. At about 3:00 AM on the 14th, while the citizens were still fast asleep, they suddenly heard loud gongs and frequent police whistles. The residents awoke from their sweet dreams, and the sky was already ablaze with fire. The area around Xishi Street resembled a fire dragon. Soon after, fire engines and fire brigades rushed to the scene, sucking water and injecting it, but because the streets were narrow, they could not get close. Moreover, a strong north wind was blowing that night, adding to the fire's intensity and speed of spread. In an instant, fires broke out in all directions. Later, the fire brigade opened a firebreak from a distance to prevent it from spreading. After several attempts to extinguish the fire, the flames were extinguished until the sky was bright (around 7:00 AM). An investigation revealed that the fire was caused by the carelessness of the Guang Hengsheng Beijing Fruit and Seafood Store on Xishi Street. When the fire broke out, six or seven shop assistants fled in confusion, but the son of an old partner, about fifteen years old, who was sleeping upstairs, was not rescued by his companions and died in the fire pit. Later, his remains were unearthed, his head and face scorched, a very tragic death. A total of 47 shops were burned down. In addition to the Guang Hengsheng store where the fire started, they included: Lianchang Pork Store, empty shops No. 1 and 2, Fengfa Tobacco Store, Qili Store, Yongchang Store, Chunshengtang Herbal Medicine Store, Ruiyuan Sundries Store, Baosheng Herbal Medicine Store, Nanzhanhao, Yongyuan Store, Caiyuan Teahouse, Lisheng Tobacco Store, Chunji Beef Store, Dahua Barber Shop, Fushan Nunnery, Lianghe Soda Store, Minzhong School, Longji Paper Store, Sanxing Salted Fish Store, Faji Fresh Fish Store, Lianan Pork Store, Rongzhen Sundries Store, You Nan Bakery, Yonghe Pawnshop, all on Xishi Main Street. The burned-down residences on Jielong Xin Street include: Wang Residence, Zhou Residence, Guangyuan Stack, Kong Residence, Yongantang on Longdao Main Street, Tongde Tobacco Store, Rongxing Stationery Store, Tongsheng Paper Store, Xingji Cloth Store, Anji Cloth Store, Dexiang Teahouse, Desheng Silver Store, Deji Cloth Store, two empty shops. Longxingsheng Preserved Meat Store on Longdao Tongjin Street, Yuanchang Earthenware Store, Baoan Incense Store, Dajisheng Lantern Store. (October 15th)

Nanjing Correspondence

Dunpan's Shadowy Words (Part 1): A Sideways Look at Sino-Japanese Diplomacy 41

Tracing the history of China and Japan, two countries that are close as lips and teeth, officials have sought peace and mutual benefit. However, since the sudden outbreak of the September 18th Incident, although diplomatic relations between the two countries have remained for five years, a practical assessment shows that the conflict has spread from the three northeastern provinces to the entire province of Rehe. Localized resistance has lasted for months. The deeper the stimulation, the greater the impact, leading to the occurrence of other unfortunate incidents. Considering the root causes, it is possible to overstate the situation. Even from the perspective of negotiation, the Executive Yuan established the Beiping Political Affairs Reorganization Committee three years ago, and the Military Affairs Commission also established a branch in Beiping. However, the situation became entangled, and the environment became increasingly pressing. The scope of exploration and discussion was limited to local events. The abolition of the Political Affairs Reorganization Committee last autumn seemed to herald an impending crisis. After several twists and turns, the Hebei-Chahar Political Affairs Committee was established. However, its limited powers and responsibilities were largely confined to local matters. As such, over the months and years, although diplomatic channels between China and Japan remained open and diplomatic organs continued to exchange visits, the mere mention of diplomatic issues evoked a sense of infinite difficulty, as if one were faced with a twenty-four-volume history, unsure of where to begin. Is this not exceedingly strange? The current adjustment of diplomatic relations between the two countries is circuitous and complex, and the future outcome is impossible for outsiders to predict. Even the negotiations of the past half month cannot be fully known due to the confidentiality period. However, this matter is of great importance to the future of the country and is something that the people eagerly want to know. Therefore, I have gathered information from the sidelines, verified old news, and offer it to the readers, knowing that I may be blamed.

The current Sino-Japanese negotiations can be broadly divided into stages A and B. Stage A encompasses the period from the Japanese proposal to the suspension of negotiations. Stage B covers the period after the suspension of negotiations, when President Chiang returned to Nanjing and Ambassador Kawagoe held talks, up to the present. Within these stages, there have also been side activities. Stage B is currently underway, and it is still too early to say whether it will proceed smoothly or encounter further complications. However, the people of the country should establish limits and uphold principles. Matters deemed worthy of discussion should not deviate from these principles; otherwise, we must politely decline. If our defenses are strong, the results will be positive, and this is something that the people should strive for together.

Let us first discuss the methods employed in stage A. Traditionally, diplomacy has involved both written and oral communication. As for adjusting diplomatic relations, oral communication is naturally the initial step for preliminary exploration. Once written words are involved, they leave traces, unlike spoken words, which allow for the mutual expression of problems, repeated questioning, and the exploration of the true nature and origins of issues. However, because oral discourse lacks definition, it is prone to contraction and expansion, and the risk of imprudent words and loss of composure is unavoidable. Moreover, there are significant differences in the importance and urgency of matters. If the oral communication does not come from a single source, it becomes even more inconsistent. The best way to respond is to strengthen one's own position and adopt a calm and firm attitude. Regardless of whether the other party is a single person or more, we can handle it calmly with a single person. We can report to the readers on the process of stage A. Both the proposals made by Japan and our responses were oral. However, the proposals made by Japan were not necessarily all voiced by a single person, while we responded with the strength of a single person.

As for the items in Japan's so-called diplomatic plan, it was initially said that there were seven, but they have not been made public, making it impossible to list them. Consulting the newspapers of both countries, as well as foreign news agencies such as Reuters, reveals varying accounts. However, the differences lie only in the addition or subtraction of items, while the main points remain the same. Now, let us discuss these main points separately and try to describe the perceptions from the standpoints of both countries. Since we belong to opposing sides, the adjustment of diplomatic relations will naturally be fraught with difficulties, and it is impossible to achieve results overnight.

Among the various items, the one most worthy of our attention is the so-called "clarification of North China." This is something that the Chinese and foreign press have been competing to report. North China and South China are merely geographical terms used casually. In reality, the provincial system is subordinate to the central government, leaving no room for any deviation. Three years ago, during the Changcheng War, the Executive Yuan established a committee in Beiping. This was a temporary measure by the government to strengthen the border defense, and it was never intended to suggest that the provinces of Hebei and Chahar required separate organizations. The establishment of a branch of the Military Affairs Commission to command military affairs was like setting up a command headquarters in each province during the suppression of the communists. There was no element of political separation involved. However, with these organizations in place, the political affairs of Hebei and Chahar, even local matters, were sometimes concentrated in the two committees. In fulfilling their duties, the two committees could not avoid limited external negotiations. As this accumulated over time, Japan came to believe that the political institutions of North China must be handled by North China itself. They even cited items from the temporary powers and responsibilities of that time, or even items that were only discussed but never implemented, claiming that since there were proposals at the time, they should be implemented urgently. They seem to be unaware that the so-called items were conceived by a small group of people and cannot be considered precedents. There is no precedent to speak of at all. Some Japanese may believe that matters negotiated above can be easily resolved at the local level, while it is difficult for the central government to make remote decisions. It is better for the central government to grant greater special powers to the local authorities, so that they can resolve matters directly, turn big issues into small ones, and come to a consensus, somewhat similar to the situation in the three northeastern provinces before 1928, where Zhang Zuolin's word was final. However, the environment is different, and the political situation has changed. Carving a mark on a boat to find a lost sword will not work. Even if it did, it would not necessarily turn big issues into small ones. Japan believes that Hebei, Chahar, and other provinces are adjacent to the northeastern provinces, and recently, economic and military activities have become increasingly frequent. They insist on the name of "clarification" to fully implement their plans. This is fundamentally different from our country's perspective. In our country, sovereignty resides in the central government, and no other country is allowed to interfere. The division of power is governed by the laws of the constitution. If the needs of the times or special circumstances require it, measures should be taken to strengthen the political institutions of the northern provinces within the principle of not losing sovereignty and adapting to the environment. How can we entrust this to the name of authorization and engage in the practice of cutting our feet to fit the shoes? This is something that the people of the country believe in and the government's policy is based on. Within Hebei Province, there is also the illegal organization of Eastern Hebei, which is even more at odds with our political system. Our side cannot remain silent on this matter.

The issue of anti-communism is widely discussed, as seen in the reports. It is considered a key point in the negotiations. The communist issue involves military actions and ideological issues. Our country's political system is fundamentally different from communism. As for communist military actions, the work of suppression in recent years has been visible to all. We have spared no effort. As for ideological issues, they belong to the realm of academic thought and should be dealt with separately, not lumped together with military affairs. However, Japan is now talking about joint anti-communism without a clear scope. This matter is purely an internal affair in which no other country should interfere. Therefore, if there is indeed an anti-communism item in the diplomatic adjustment plan, we hope that those who speak on it will adopt a cautious attitude, lest it cause further irritation and make people suspect that the professed anti-communism is a disguise for interfering in our internal politics.

The tariff issue is also a major aspect of this matter. Our country has been constrained by treaty tariffs for many years. After several negotiations, we have finally managed to free ourselves from the shackles and seek autonomy. However, compared to the barriers erected by other countries, we still feel weak. Since last winter, the Japanese have been engaged in smuggling on a large scale, shipping goods to Hebei Province from Korea without regard for distance, openly transporting goods and resisting with force. On the one hand, they are skillfully creating the name of special trade; on the other hand, they are claiming that reducing taxes will prosper the market, in order to clear out the backlog of their industrial products. Japan relies on industry to build the nation, but it also lacks raw materials. The key to its success lies in the low cost of its manufacturing and its sales in the world market. If it relies on its scientific skills and low labor costs to sell its goods in the world market through competition, this is the right way of trade. However, to force others to reduce taxes to increase their sales, to use smuggling as a means of coercing tax reductions, and to further break our principle of autonomous tariffs, forcing us to return to the shackles that we have already escaped, this is not a reasonable matter. The principle of autonomy has been fought for through hardships, and no one is willing to return to the shackles to weaken their national power. Therefore, it is right for us to reject this and at the same time contain smuggling as a countermeasure.

Li Sihao Added to the Hebei-Chahar Economic Committee, Shen Nengyi Has Arrived in Beiping and Will Assume a New Position, Beiping Banking Circles Host Banquet for Li and Zhang Shizhao 42

(Beiping) After Li Sihao took office as Chairman of the Economic Committee, he did not make many changes to the committee's staff. It is reported that Li will add several new members to the committee, including Shen Nengyi, former Director of the Printing Bureau of the Ministry of Finance, who has already arrived in Beiping. However, he has declined many visitors. Furthermore, Li Sihao is scheduled to go to Tianjin on the 18th to exchange views with various parties on the development of the North China economy. He will return to Beiping after staying for a few days. The Beiping banking circles are scheduled to host a banquet for Li and Zhang Shizhao on the evening of the 17th, and many dignitaries have been invited to attend. (17th Dispatch from Central News Agency)

National Economic Construction Movement and Promoting Agricultural and Forestry Production Construction 43

— Zeng Jikuan

At present, China's rural economy is bankrupt, the people's lives are difficult, and the future of the nation is precarious. The only urgent problem is how to increase production and revive the countryside, so that the people can rest and recuperate, and work together in the national economic construction movement, moving towards the general goal of "exhausting human power, developing land resources, balancing supply and demand, and facilitating circulation to seek the healthy development of the national economy," in order to achieve the goal of national rejuvenation. Therefore, in view of the future trend of economic construction in Jiangsu Province, we will focus on the application of scientific and technological methods to promote the construction of various agricultural and forestry productions. Since this is inextricably linked to the national economic construction movement, I will briefly state my humble opinions on the key points of their interdependence for exploration.

In simple terms, the National Economic Construction Movement is a poverty alleviation movement, which is also a national salvation or national rejuvenation movement. Sun Yat-sen said: "The most important thing in construction is the people's livelihood. People's livelihood is the life of the people, the survival of the country, the livelihood of the society, and the life of the masses." It is also the lifeblood of the national economy. The development of the national economy will lead to the prosperity of the people's livelihood; the suffering of the people's livelihood will lead to the decline of the national economy. It can be seen that the significance of the national economic construction movement lies in arousing the national consciousness and uniting the strength of the entire nation to fight for national salvation. This is different from the struggle for survival of ordinary people. This is to cultivate people's strength in a planned and organized manner, to use people's strength to engage in various production and construction movements, so as to promote the healthy development of the national economy. It is not like the economic activities of individuals, which are merely unconscious, selfish, and self-interested production behaviors.

Now that we deeply understand the true meaning of the National Economic Construction Movement, we should further discuss the methods and steps for implementing the National Economic Construction Movement. Although the methods are nothing more than utilizing the cooperative system, the education system, the military organization, the cooperation of academic institutions and academic groups, or the automation of industrial groups and production organizations themselves, the most important thing in the implementation steps is to actively engage in agricultural and forestry production and construction movements. The reason is that the foundation of our country's national economy is in the countryside. The decline in agricultural and forestry production will lead to the decline of the rural economy, and the national economy will also decline. Therefore, our country's human and financial resources are showing a scattered and disorganized phenomenon. Therefore, if we want to promote the prosperity of the rural economy, we must actively improve agricultural and forestry production. However, if we want to increase national wealth, improve the people's lives, and seek the healthy development of the national economy, we must first seek the self-sufficiency of our country's agricultural and forestry products. Due to the impact of international imperialism's economic aggression, our country's production cannot be self-sufficient. If we want to achieve the goal of universal improvement of agricultural and forestry production and preserve the lifeblood of our country's national economy, the whole country must work together from top to bottom to carry out the rural revitalization movement. In other words, without the national strength of the entire country engaged in the national economic construction movement, it is not enough to solve the problem of increasing production and reviving the countryside.

In recent years, due to the backwardness of our country's production, the forces of international capitalism have invaded our country's agriculture, and farmers have suffered from economic oppression, which has been enough to destroy the vitality of Chinese agriculture. Tracing its origins, it is due to the fact that our country's agricultural and forestry production and construction are too immature and lack a sound organization. There is a regret that people have not done their best and the land has not been fully utilized. If we want to remedy its shortcomings and promote agricultural and forestry production and construction, its organization and steps must be unified. However, this requires the joint efforts of the people, which is even more urgent. Therefore, all agricultural and forestry production and construction projects must be carried out through the entire national economic construction movement in order to exert their grand effects and lay the initial foundation for the rejuvenation of the nation.

Taking the promotion of reclamation and cultivation as an example, the development of reclamation and cultivation must rely on the promotion of agricultural cooperation. The use of cooperative organizations can collectivize farmland, mechanize tools, and combine purchasing and sales. The collectivization of farmland can avoid the drawbacks of overlapping ridges, small areas, and irregular terrain, and implement land consolidation suitable for the scale of operation. It can also use agricultural machinery to improve planting and achieve the purpose of increasing production. The joint purchase and sale can enable farmers to obtain cheap seeds and fertilizers, reduce production costs, and sell products at high prices, avoiding the exploitation and unnecessary consumption of merchants in the middle. However, agricultural cooperative undertakings are helpful to the progress of reclamation undertakings, and the joint efforts of the people are indispensable. The coastal reclamation area of northern Jiangsu Province is vast, with more than six million mu of arable but uncultivated grassland. If we want to develop it in the future to enrich people's lives, the first step is to use agricultural cooperation to concentrate the people near the reclamation area on a common goal, that is, the national economic construction movement. Reclamation is a long-term plan and must be done by combining the efforts of the group to succeed. As for the promotion of cooperative undertakings, various social figures must use each other. Only when the insightful and perceptive people who have conducted in-depth research on cooperative undertakings advocate it, and the later-knowing and later-perceptive people lack effective publicity, can the implementation power of the ignorant and unaware masses be concentrated, and the optimistic success of the undertakings be expected. If we devote ourselves to the National Economic Construction Movement, then what the insightful and perceptive people advocate and invent will be promoted by the efforts of the later-knowing and later-perceptive people, and the ignorant and unaware people will do their best to complete it happily. Not only can cooperative undertakings be promoted smoothly, but also all reclamation work can be carried out by combining the efforts of the group.

The construction of agricultural irrigation works must also have a common organization of the people to be promoted effectively. Irrigation works are the key to transportation and irrigation, and disaster prevention. If the harbors are silted up and the drainage is not smooth, floods will inevitably occur in the event of heavy rain, and agricultural production will not be successful. Last year, the flood disaster affected the north and the south. Jiangsu Province was spared from the flood disaster, which was not the obvious effect of the government and the people working together on water conservancy construction. It can be seen that agricultural irrigation works require the sincere cooperation of the people and wealth to fundamentally prevent and control disasters and increase production effects. If so, then it is necessary to arouse the people to have a common understanding of the National Economic Construction Movement in order to increase their interest in engaging in production and construction.

Forestry directly affects the supply of industrial raw materials, and indirectly relates to the prevention and control of water and drought disasters, occupying the most important position in the National Economic Construction. However, its effect is slow to appear and lasts for a long time. Moreover, large-scale afforestation throughout the country is not enough to exert direct and indirect effects. In addition, newly planted young forests and naturally grown trees are scattered in mountains and fields everywhere, making management difficult. It is difficult to improve the knowledge of forestry cooperation among the local people and to improve their awareness of forest protection. If we want the people of the whole country to work hard on afforestation and actively protect forests, it is difficult to achieve effective results by relying only on the frequent promulgation of government decrees and the supervision of officials. It is only by regulating the closely related people's strength and wealth under the National Economic Construction Movement that it can be called upon to promote the development of forestry.

The prevention and control of diseases and insect pests of agricultural and forestry crops also requires the common consensus of all regions. Diseases and insect pests of crops and forests spread very quickly, especially insect pests. It is difficult to achieve effective results by implementing prevention and control methods only in one region or one place. We must contact all relevant parties to mobilize the whole body and eliminate them at the same time to have the possibility of fundamental elimination. The rural people in various places lack knowledge of disease and pest control. When diseases and insect pests occur in the vicinity, they are indifferent and watch from the sidelines. In order to reduce the diseases and insect pests of agricultural and forestry crops in various places and seek to increase production, we must first arouse the people in various places to carry out the movement of disease and pest control. If we want to achieve this goal, we must first devote ourselves to the National Economic Construction Movement to promote their common relationship.

To carry out agricultural extension, we must penetrate into the countryside and improve agricultural and forestry production. In particular, the producers must be willing to accept guidance in order to achieve twice the result with half the effort. The agricultural and forestry institutions established by the government employ specialized talents. After years of trial and research, there are excellent seeds and planting methods that can be promoted. However, if we want the farmers who produce to be willing to accept them, and these good seeds and methods can be promoted universally, we cannot rely solely on the power of administration. We must use cooperative farming methods to implement large-scale promotion campaigns. To implement large-scale promotion campaigns, we must concentrate on the common goal of the National Economic Construction Movement and devote all our efforts to penetrating into the countryside in order to achieve the goal of improving agriculture and increasing production.

In summary, the human and material resources that rely on the promotion of the above points must have an appropriately used organization. In particular, industrial groups and production institutions must cooperate to take the agricultural and forestry production and construction movement as the vanguard and the National Economic Construction Movement as the general driving force, unite all sectors of the community, the entire people, pool their wisdom and efforts, divide the work and cooperate, and work hard towards the same general goal. Then, we can reach the final stage of national economic construction, and the foundation of national rejuvenation will be further consolidated.

Current Affairs Commentary

The Background and Impact of Belgium's Declaration of Neutrality 44

— Hua

The King of Belgium convened a plenary meeting of the cabinet the other day. He declared that Belgium would restore its pre-war policy of neutrality. The significance of this declaration is equivalent to Belgium's statement that it abandons its responsibilities under the Locarno Treaty and the Franco-Belgian military agreement of 1920. At a time when several fascist ambitious countries in Europe are running rampant and continuously striking at the collective security system, Belgium's change of policy will obviously have serious implications. The French government has now raised questions. Although the British authorities are keeping silent, the public clearly expresses no small amount of shock. Even the entire diplomatic community in Europe will have to readjust its policies because of this sudden change. We should understand the background and possible impact of this important change in international relations.

There are two aspects to the King of Belgium's announcement of the restoration of the pre-war Chinese policy this time. One is domestic and the other is international. Domestically, we can see the reasons for this change from the foreign policies of the two main ethnic groups in Belgium. Originally, the Belgian people mainly belong to two ethnic groups. The Walloons are mostly near France, and the Flemings are mostly near the Netherlands. The Walloons speak French and the Flemings speak Dutch. They have a big difference in their policy towards France. The Walloons advocate being pro-French, while the Flemings oppose being pro-French and advocate the same as the Netherlands, with British power as a security guarantee. After the European War, in view of the past war's disaster, the country proposed to Britain to conclude a military alliance, but it was unsuccessful due to various reasons. In 1920, Belgium concluded a military alliance with France. This alliance was regarded as a great victory for the Walloons, but the Flemings always insisted on opposing it. However, in the past ten years after the war, France seemed to become the leader of the European continent, and its alliance with Belgium did not shake in the slightest because of the Flemings' opposition. But in the past two years, there have been changes in two situations that have gradually given the anti-French faction an advantage. One is that Hitler has continuously broken the Treaty of Versailles, torn up the Locarno Treaty, and expanded the navy, army and air force. France has not adopted a strong policy to deal with it. This indicates that France's hegemony on the mainland has been declining, and some pro-French Belgians have also begun to waver. The other is that after the Franco-Soviet Mutual Assistance Treaty was established, the conservative reactionaries in Belgium had doubts about France. Suspecting that the Flemings' anti-French policy suddenly increased many supporters. Since the establishment of the Dutch cabinet after the election in May of this year, the so-called "completely independent" foreign policy has already revealed the signs of alienating France. It was expected in the international community that the King of Belgium would announce a change of policy now.

Regarding the international background, both Britain and Germany are not without relationships. Britain's jealousy of France's hegemony on the mainland has not changed in the past ten years after the war. His alliance with Germany and Italy to contain France changed once when Italy invaded Abyssinia, but it was very temporary. When the Italo-Ethiopian War ended, Britain's tolerance of Germany's aggressive policy was as obvious as before. Therefore, for the future Locarno Five-Power Conference, Britain has tried its best to make France yield to Germany. And this time, Belgium's restoration of the pre-war policy of neutrality may have been influenced by Britain. According to foreign news reports, keen observers believe that the King's declaration this time was agreed with the British government in advance. This has been denied by powerful parties in London. However, the reaction of the British Conservative Party newspapers to this incident shows "sympathetic" understanding, and clues can be found. The Belgian people will never have a good impression of Germany. But since May of this year, a Rexist Party has newly appeared in Belgium, led by a young lawyer, Degrelle. His tendency is similar to that of the German National Socialist Party. This certainly cannot be proven to mean that the Rexist Party has relations with Germany. But the German National Socialist Party's attempt to invade Belgium has been very fierce in recent years. As long as Belgium remains conservatively neutral, it will be beneficial to Germany's aggressive policies.

The most urgent impact of this change in Belgium's foreign policy is the weakening of the defense of the northern border of France, which strengthens Germany's threat to France. Therefore, it is natural that Berlin expressed satisfaction with the King's announcement. As for the long-term impact, the European collective security system has suffered a serious blow. Even if Belgium does not take further steps to withdraw from the League of Nations, it has at least retreated to a passive position of inaction on the current world's "indivisible" peace movement. The crisis of European war in the future will therefore be even closer.

Spanish Rebels Advance Rapidly Towards the Capital, Madrid's Defense Outer Line Shakes, Government Troops Actively Prepare to Defend the City 46

Navalcarnero, the Spanish government forces were defeated by the rebels' fierce artillery fire today, and are now retreating. Once this city falls, the outer line of Madrid's defense will collapse. (16th National News Agency Telegram)

Daravanra, a special dispatch from our reporter: The troops commanded by General Varela of the National Army launched an attack on the city of Madrid this afternoon and immediately occupied the town of Valmoyeada, which is in front of the city of Navalcarnero. Once the city of Navalcarnero is captured, they can directly attack the capital. In today's battle, the National Army advanced six kilometers first and did not encounter strong resistance. Later, it was swept by government troops with machine guns in Qian Qian, and then stabbed with bayonets, and finally defeated the government troops. The government troops also abandoned many corpses, it is said. (16th Havas Telegram)

Madrid, the government troops are now retreating along the 35-mile line. The rebels surrounding the capital can advance very quickly. Navalcarnero, the last fortress outside Madrid, is in danger of falling at any time. The rebel column led by General Varela is now only five miles away from the town. Although the defensive works there are solid, they are afraid that it will be difficult to resist the rebels who are full of combat experience and commanded by good generals to repeatedly attack. If the rebels capture the town, it will be the first major victory in the western invasion of Madrid, and then they can attack the capital from the northwest. General Varela personally supervised the battle today and captured Valmojacada, the last village before the town of Navalcarnero. The rebels started from Santa Cruz Tritaema near the dawn, with the columns commanded by Colonel Yacob and General Asensio on both wings as escorts. The rebels did not encounter any resistance at first, but when they advanced to four miles from the village, the government troops bombarded fiercely with guns and cannons, and bullets rained down. General Varela's elite troops charged with bayonets, and before they reached the trenches guarded by the government troops, the government troops had fled, abandoning two field guns and many machine guns. The rebels then entered the village from the north and south sides and advanced ten miles towards the capital. The rebels are also engaged in a roundabout attack further north on the town of Escorial, 30 miles from the capital, which is connected by a well-built highway. Once the town falls, the rebels can attack the rear of the government troops' northern defense line. It is now heard that the capital is actively preparing for the defense of the city, digging trenches at various key points, and solid houses are being converted into small blockhouses. (17th Reuters Telegram)

(Tokyo) Regarding the issue of establishing two committees to determine the border and to deal with the border disputes between the Soviet Union and Manchuria, Japan has consulted with "Manchukuo" and submitted a counter-proposal to the Soviet government. Ambassador Yurenev visited Foreign Minister Arita in the afternoon of the 16th, according to the instructions of his home government, and also submitted the Soviet counter-proposal in official documents. On that day, Ambassador Yurenev first reiterated his long-standing claim, that is, (1) Although the mixed committee for handling border disputes agrees to first set up the Japanese-Manchurian case in the eastern border (from Xingkai Lake to Tumen River), the mixed committee for determining the border must initially aim at determining the entire border between the Soviet Union and Manchuria. (2) Before the two mixed committees for determining the border are set up, in order to ensure the peace of the border, it is necessary to take appropriate measures. At the same time, the Soviet counter-proposal was submitted to the Soviet side in official documents (Russian), explaining its contents item by item. Before the entire explanation was completed, the bell rang six times, and he took his leave. It was decided to meet again next week. The Soviet side will submit a proposal explaining the contents in English and continue to discuss it. After the Soviet side completes its explanation at the meeting next week, the Japanese Director-General of the European and Asian Affairs Bureau, Togo, and the Soviet Counselor, Levedev, will open a special committee to continue the discussion based on the Japanese-Manchurian and Soviet cases. US Presidential Election Enters Final Stage: Roosevelt Criticizes New York Banking Circles, Landon to Invade California 53

(New York) With the presidential election drawing near, the activities of the presidential candidates from various parties are becoming increasingly active. President Roosevelt has completed his 5,000-mile trip from Denver to Detroit and returned to New York. Republican presidential candidate Landon, after returning to Kansas, made a surprising move, suddenly telling reporters that he had decided to extend his influence to California and hoped to gain the state's support. Smith, the former Democratic presidential candidate who recently broke away from the Democratic Party, plans to meet with Landon at the end of the month in New York to discuss the wording of the final major campaign speech. Socialist presidential candidate Thomas predicts that President Roosevelt will be re-elected, saying, "It is not my personal wish that he be elected, but the people will all vote for Roosevelt." (16th Reuters)

Creeven - President Roosevelt spoke to 40,000 listeners from the rear platform of a special train today, vigorously criticizing the anti-government propaganda of New York banking circles, saying that a kind of propaganda is now being spread from the New York financial center to stockbrokers across the country against his re-election. The expenses for this propaganda are all provided by these stockbrokers, but by the third of next month, ordinary merchants and investors will be able to show that they have not been fooled. (16th National News)

Wilmington - Today, Senator Cuffee, chairman of the Democratic Senate Committee, announced in New York that Republican presidential candidate Landon's campaign expenses had received a large donation from the famous DuPont family, totaling $583,000. Cuffee also said that he had predicted that the DuPont family would donate up to $750,000 to the Republican Party during the election. After investigation, he felt that this statement was even more credible. The two DuPont brothers are very wealthy Americans. In the 1932 presidential election, the brothers were political enemies, with the elder brother supporting Hoover and the younger brother supporting Roosevelt. (16th Reuters)

Topeka - Republican presidential candidate Landon announced here today, during the heated presidential election competition, that he would rush to Los Angeles on the 20th of this month to give a speech, so that California would vote to support the Republican Party. Observers believe that Landon's entry into the West, as an important campaign strategy, is enough to increase Landon's prestige. (16th National News)

Philadelphia - After President Roosevelt delivered a campaign speech the other day, accusing the Republican Party of being responsible for the economic panic, former President Hoover gave a speech here in response, briefly stating that the economic panic was the result of the European War and no one could be held responsible. As for the economic recovery, whether in the United States or around the world, signs had appeared nine months before President Roosevelt was elected, and it was not due to the current government. The budget figures presented by President Roosevelt are huge and the payments are excessive. "If the accounting books of private enterprises were similar to the current government's budget, those in charge would certainly have been imprisoned." (16th Havas)

First Air Defense Drill in Paris After European War: Sirens Sounded in 70 Places, City in Darkness for One Hour 59

(Paris) The entire city of Paris was in darkness for one hour tonight. This was the first air defense drill after the European War. First, sirens sounded in the four cities, and powerful searchlight beams swept back and forth in the sky. All vehicles in the city stopped immediately, and military and civilian groups worked hard together to resist enemy aircraft attacks. Anti-aircraft guns fired loudly everywhere, and fire brigades rushed to put out the simulated fires. Rescue teams rushed to rescue the simulated bombing sites, and anti-gas teams rushed to the sites where enemy aircraft released poison gas to provide relief. Several fighter planes in the air intercepted the enemy aircraft. (16th National News)

(Paris) Here last night there was a slight fog, and sparse starlight peeked out from the clouds, swaying uncertainly. The passive air defense drill was carried out on time in the twilight according to the planned schedule. This was still the first time since the European War. At 9:20 p.m., the sirens of more than 70 factories sounded, warning the entire city to turn off the lights. At the same time, all vehicles on the street also stopped. At 9:43 p.m., several large bombers circled over the Pantheon and dropped huge flames as a symbol of bombs. One bomb fell at the foot of Rousseau's statue. Nurses throughout the city put on special clothing and put on gas masks and immediately set out to rescue. Firefighters also carried various washing and disinfecting materials and rushed to the scene after hearing the alarm. Subsequently, two bombs also fell near the statue of the 17th-century playwright Corneille and the Odéon Theater. The anti-aircraft artillery team immediately fired back, and fires broke out everywhere (imaginary), and firefighters rushed to put them out, which was very tense. Soon the fire was extinguished. At 12:30 midnight, the enemy aircraft escaped, and the entire city was lifted from martial law. All streets immediately returned to normal. According to the police chief Langeron, the situation in each district was very good. However, at the beginning of the exercise, more than 40 people lit flames, intending to take the opportunity to demonstrate. They were dispersed by the police and 11 people were arrested. Some anarchists distributed rebellious leaflets and were also arrested by the police. As for those who were charged with violating the law for not turning off the lights immediately, there were 458 cases. (17th Havas)

(Paris) Paris held an air defense drill last night, but it was declared a failure because the public failed to fully accept police instructions. According to the plan, Paris should have become pitch black, but some Parisians regarded this as a joke and instead formed teams to patrol the streets, singing folk songs. Some anarchists even lit fires at street corners to play pranks, so this drill was declared a failure. (17th National News)

(Tokyo) The situation of Japan's cotton cloth exports is not as satisfactory as expected this spring. Both the quantity and value have shown a downward trend. Guizhou Province Moves Its Government: All Agencies in Nanning Relocated to Guilin; Guilin Headquarters of the Guizhou Army Established; Cai Tingkai's Troops to Be Consolidated into One Division 65

Guangzhou Dispatch: Chen Cheng, the Chief of Staff of the Guangzhou Military Affairs Commission, recently went to Guizhou to discuss military affairs with Li Bai. After participating in the inspection of the Guizhou Army in Guilin, he immediately returned to Guangdong and then went north to report to Chairman Chiang. It is said that Chen's visit to Guizhou was to discuss the reorganization of the Guizhou Army, which will likely remain based on its original establishment but with a change of designations. As for the number of troops, it will remain at six divisions, or special units may be added. Once approved by the Central Government, an official announcement will be made. Troop demobilization has been underway for several days, and it is said that the Central Government has initially allocated 300,000 yuan for relocation expenses. The monthly military subsidy will be remitted to Guizhou starting this month. The incorporation of Cai Tingkai's army into the Fifth Route Army of Guizhou is currently in progress. The three division commanders, Weng Zhaoyuan, Qu Shounian, and Qiu Zhaochen, went to Nanning to meet Bai and discuss the method of incorporation. Bai therefore flew to Guilin on the 12th to discuss the matter in detail with Li Zongren. It is found that although Cai's army stationed in Guizhou has three division headquarters in Nanning—the 60th, 61st, and 78th divisions—the actual number of troops, when combined, is less than one division. Qu Shounian's unit has only seven companies, and Qiu and Weng's units together have no more than sixteen or seventeen companies. They are still stationed separately in Yulin, Bobai, and other places and have not moved. The three units will be consolidated into one division and incorporated into the Guizhou Army. The choice of division commander has not yet been determined. It may be selected from among Qu Shounian, Weng Zhaoyuan, Qiu Zhaochen, and Dai Ji. It is rumored that Qu and Dai have a higher chance, while Qiu and Weng may have other assignments. Guizhou Province moved its provincial capital to Guilin, and currently, all agencies in Nanning have been relocated in order. The first to move was the provincial government. Currently, all departments are working together in the same building. The Provincial Public Security Bureau has also moved to Guilin. The matters handled by the Nanning Public Security Bureau were transferred to the Yongning County Government on the 7th. The Special Party Headquarters of the Guizhou Army Headquarters also moved to Guilin on the 7th. It is estimated that starting from the 1st of this month, the military, political, and party agencies in Nanning have been relocated one after another. Documents and files were transported to Guilin by car, while bulky items were transported by more than a hundred civilian boats via the Fu River. Provincial government employees were given relocation subsidies due to the move. Appointed officials received a travel allowance of 100 yuan each, recommended officials received 80 yuan, and delegated officials were divided into three levels: 60 yuan, 40 yuan, and 20 yuan. After the relocation, Nanning suddenly had tens of thousands fewer agency employees residing there, and rents therefore fell sharply. Rents that were previously 50 yuan per month have now fallen to 20 yuan, due to the oversupply of housing. Speculative merchants are also preparing to move their shops to Guilin. Therefore, the current situation in Nanning has a feeling of the past. What remains is only the Nanning Military Academy. The original Guizhou Army Headquarters has been changed to an forward command post, with Xia Wei, the commander of the 15th Army of the Guizhou Army, as the director of the Nanning forward command post. The forward command post is organized into seven sections, with Huang Shaoping appointed as the director of the Transportation Section, Liu Fuqin as the director of the Ordnance Section, Wu Bingquan as the director of the Military Affairs Section, Mo Dongxi as the director of the Military Law Section, Li Bingzhong as the director of the Military Transportation Section, and Huang Yin as the director of the Military Medical Section. It began operations on the 11th of this month. After the provincial capital moved to Guilin, the security of southeastern Guizhou Province is entirely maintained by the militia. Due to the vast area of the southeast, in addition to strengthening the militia force, the Yulin area has been separated from the Xunzhou Militia Command Area to establish the Yulin Militia Command Area. Luo Zhen, the deputy commander of the Xunzhou area, was transferred to fill the position of commander of the Yulin Militia. The Yulin Command was established on Double Ten Day. (October 14)

Soaring Grain Prices in Bengbu: Scarce Supply Cannot Meet Demand; Wheat and Soybean Prices Rise Steadily 67

Bengbu Dispatch: In northern Anhui, wheat and soybeans are the main agricultural products. This year, the counties have had a bumper harvest, with particularly large yields. The rural economy has improved, and farmers have had a chance to recover. The majority of these large quantities of agricultural products, aside from a small portion used for local consumption, are concentrated in Bengbu and then transported to Xihu, Tianjin, and other places. In addition, a significant amount of agricultural products from eastern Henan are also transported here for resale to other provinces. During the summer and autumn this year, the grain market in Bengbu was quite active. After the Jinpu Railway Bureau reduced freight rates for soybeans, sales of Anhui soybeans became even more brisk. In addition, imports of soybeans were scarce this autumn, causing soybean prices in Shanghai to gradually increase. Recently, the supply of soybeans has been relatively scarce, and there is a shortage of vehicles on the Jinpu Railway, making transportation difficult. Grain merchants are sitting idly by, unable to buy soybeans or find vehicles to transport them. Under the circumstances of supply not meeting demand, soybean prices have been soaring. Recently, the market price of large yellow soybeans from Yingzhou has risen from 14 yuan to 14.3 or 14.4 yuan per shi. Even medium-sized yellow soybeans have risen from 13.8 yuan to 14 yuan. Based on current observations, soybean prices are still expected to rise. The situation in the wheat market is similar, with scarce supply and prices not meeting demand. The Bengbu-based agents of flour mills in the north and south, as well as general grain merchants, have had no goods to buy in recent days. The only transactions are small amounts. There are few grain boats on the river, and the grain market is quiet. Grain stores have no business to do and are secretly complaining. The soaring wheat prices are particularly alarming. Feihe flower wheat has risen to 16.4 yuan per shi, Shouzhou red wheat to 15.8 yuan per shi, and Yingzhou white wheat to 15.6 yuan per shi, an increase of one yuan per shi compared to a few days ago. While soaring grain prices are sufficient to improve the rural economy, they are also having a significant impact on the livelihoods of city residents. (October 15)

Changshu: Determination of Crop Quality for Autumn Harvest 72

In order to determine the quality of the autumn harvest here, the Provincial Department of Finance specially sent Lu Lianjie to Changshu to conduct an inspection. After four or five days of inspecting various rural areas, he determined that the harvest was abundant. On the afternoon of the 16th, he convened a meeting with the directors of the Taxation Office and the East and West Grain Bureaus, the district chiefs, and the chiefs of the Second Sections to discuss the matter. It was decided that the first and third districts would be assessed at 96.6%, the second and fourth districts at 95%, the fifth and sixth districts at 65%, and the eighth district at 70%. As for the seventh district, Dongke, it would be assessed at 91%. The overall average crop quality for cotton and rice was calculated to be 86.5%. The county magistrate and the provincial commission will now jointly submit a report to the Provincial Department for review and approval.

Tragedy of a Hacked Wife 74

Qi Junqing, a resident of Tianjin, aged 24, residing at No. 7 Maoxin Lane, Yinglong Town, outside the West Gate, used to be a printing worker in Tianjin but is now unemployed. In July of this year, he brought his wife, Lu (aged 23), to Wuxi. Lu worked as a female worker in the Shenxin Yarn Factory, while Junqing was unemployed at home due to stomach pain. On the 16th, the couple suddenly had a quarrel for some unknown reason. Lu left in anger and did not return until 11:00 PM. Lu had recently separated from her husband due to his illness and lived with her cousin, Zhang Yuelan (also known as Yu Lan), next to the stove downstairs, while Junqing lived upstairs with his relatives Zhang Jin Yuan. Yesterday (the 17th), at 6:00 AM, Lu and Yu Lan got up, and Wang Lan went to work at the factory. Lu was in the kitchen cooking noodles. At around 7:00 AM, Zhang Jin Yuan and others got up and went to the kitchen to eat noodles. Suddenly, they saw Lu lying on the ground, covered in blood, with a fatal knife wound on her neck. There was a kitchen knife next to her. Zhang shouted loudly and tried to take the injured person to the hospital, but she had already died. Later, the neighbors reported the incident to the Fourth Public Security Bureau, which sent police to investigate. The police took the deceased's husband, Qi Junqing, and Zhang Yuelan, and Zhang's mother, Li, into the Fourth Public Security Bureau for questioning. Qi Junqing remained calm and gave cunning statements. During the questioning of Zhang Yuelan, she initially claimed to know nothing, but after further interrogation, she confessed that her cousin, Qi Junqing, had gotten up and gone downstairs at around 4:00 AM this morning. She then heard a loud fight, but she didn't dare to say anything. Soon after, her cousin came upstairs, covered in blood. She asked him why he killed her cousin's wife, and he told her not to make a sound. Finally, Zhang's mother, Li, also confessed that Qi Junqing and his wife had always been at odds with each other. After the questioning, they were all detained. At around 2:00 PM, prosecutor Huang Yan, led officials to conduct an autopsy, which confirmed that the deceased was first beaten and then killed. He then ordered the village chief to prepare a coffin and report the case to the court for filing. Prosecutor Huang immediately went to the Fourth Public Security Bureau to summon neighbors and the head of the baojia system to the bureau for questioning before transferring them to the court for further investigation. It is rumored that Qi Junqing and Zhang Yuelan were having an affair, and because of the deceased Lu's knowledge, they committed this heinous crime of murdering his wife.

Changzhou: Large Quantity of Smuggled Earthenware Seized 75

Based on confidential reports, the First Public Security Bureau of Wuyi County learned that Jiang Lantian, a resident of Dong'an in the Ninth District, was a well-known earthenware smuggler. Police Chief Zhang Xingda investigated and learned that the smuggler had returned to Changzhou from Shanghai with earthenware on the 14th of this month. He waited at the station but found nothing after searching Jiang Lantian. He then released him. Later, he investigated the wharves and other places and learned that another woman had secretly transported a large quantity of smuggled earthenware to Dong'an Town. That night, he went to the town to search and found 63 packages of smuggled earthenware, large and small, on a ferry boat, as well as the boat owner, Dai Sanda, and others. The smuggler Jiang Lantian was also apprehended in the city, and the woman who delivered the earthenware, Wu Yan, was also arrested. The witnesses were escorted to the city at around 1:00 PM on the 16th. After a preliminary interrogation by Division Chief Si Daoping, Jiang Lantian confessed to the details of his previous trips to Shanghai to purchase earthenware. The others were also interrogated separately. Their confessions were recorded and they were sent to the County Public Security Bureau for further interrogation.

Taicang: Flower Field Rent Prices Agreed Upon 76

The rent prices for flower fields in this county for the 25th year of the Republic have been agreed upon at a meeting convened by the county government with tenants from various districts. The first-class rented area is 3.19 yuan per shi, the first-class rent price is 2 yuan per shi, the second-class rent price is 2.85 yuan per shi, and the fourth-class rent price is 2.7 yuan per shi. For fields outside of Haicheng, the rent price is reduced by 20 cents per shi compared to the original rent price. The old price is increased by 60 cents per shi, and there is an additional 10% charge. For payments made between November 1st and 15th, there is an additional charge of 10 cents per shi. For payments made between the 16th and 30th, there is an additional charge of 20 cents per shi. For payments made between December 1st and 15th, there is an additional charge of 30 cents per shi.

Nantong: Large Quantities of Nantong Cotton Transported to Shanghai 77

The cotton harvest in Nantong and the coastal reclamation area this year is estimated to be about one million shi of ginned cotton. Since the cotton gins in the villages opened in the middle of last month, there has been a surge of cotton. In recent days, large quantities have been exported to Shanghai. The Nantong-Shanghai riverboats have even added special trips to transport cotton clothing. More than 300,000 bales have already been transported. Currently, the cotton market is expected to decline due to rumors in Shanghai. The price of ginned cotton is 49 yuan per shi.

Doctors Assembled and Sent to Plague Area 78

A severe epidemic is raging in the northern part of Nantong, with an increasing number of deaths. On the 16th, the Epidemic Prevention Committee assembled more than 50 doctors from various hospitals and sent them to the plague area with medicines to provide treatment.

Yangzhou: Paralysis Discovered in the County Seat 79

In recent weeks, malaria and dysentery have been prevalent in Yangzhou, but fortunately, they are not very severe, and few people have died. Recently, however, a strange and dangerous disease has been discovered. It starts with paralysis throughout the body, and death occurs within 24 hours. The symptoms of the deceased include blood gushing from the mouth and nose. The Tuina Research Association, because the disease has not been seen before, does not know where to start. It has issued an emergency notice, scheduled to hold a meeting on the afternoon of the 18th to discuss treatment methods. In addition to notifying members of the association, many Chinese and Western doctors have received the notice.

Gaoyou: Disaster in Seventh and Eighth Districts 80

The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance has ordered Liu Shixiang, the accounting director of Jiangdu County, to come to Gaoyou to conduct an on-site inspection of the disaster situation in the Seventh and Eighth Districts of Huxi County. It is estimated that the average disaster rate in Helai and other villages in the Seventh District is 30%, and the average disaster rate in Ping'a and other five villages in the Eighth District is 40%.

Ningbo: Theater Performance in Zhenhai Causes Disaster 81

Every year, the Beita Temple in Meidong Township, Zhenhai, holds a theater performance to thank the gods. This year, the performance was held again on the 15th. Farmers from far and wide came to watch, crowding the roads. The temple was already old, and the spectators crowded onto the stage, causing the weight to be too much. The stage suddenly collapsed, causing chaos. People shouted for help and trampled on each other. Many women and children were injured, bleeding from their heads. Among the injured were an old man in his seventies and a young child, both of whom were barely breathing and in critical condition.

Shaoxing: District Meetings on Labor Service 82

The Construction Department of the provincial government has determined that the winter national labor service in Shaoxing this year will be for provincial water conservancy projects, specifically the repairing of three sections of seawalls: the Shaoxing section, the Xiaoshan Linpu to Huzhaoshan section, and the Yangjiatang Chejiapu section. However, the local construction projects in this county have not yet been determined. On the 14th, the county government determined the dates for district meetings: (1) the urban district on the 26th, (2) the Zhapu district on the 27th, (3) the Dongguan district on the 28th, (4) the Nanchi district on the 29th, (5) the Keqiao district on the 30th, and (6) the Anchang district on the 31st. On the scheduled dates, the district chiefs will convene meetings of the township chiefs to decide on local construction and water conservancy projects, in order to start the work as soon as possible.

Xiaoshan: Shaoxing Lacking Food 83

Zhejiang Province has always been short of food. Every year during the period between harvests, rice merchants raise prices, and then lower prices in the fall, hurting farmers. According to those familiar with the food situation, only 12 of the 75 counties in Zhejiang, namely Jiaxing and Huzhou, have a slight surplus of food annually. The remaining 63 counties are not self-sufficient. For example, the production of the seven counties in Shaoxing is 5,150,000 shi, while the demand is 7,850,000 shi, a shortfall of 2,700,000 shi. Even in a year of good harvest like this year in Xiaoshan, it still relies on neighboring counties for food. If there is a famine, the amount of rice shortage will be alarming.

Disaster Victims Cause Trouble in Villages 84

On the evening of the 14th, a large group of disaster victims suddenly came to villages such as Dongdun, Anchang, and Xizhuang, carrying baskets and burdens, speaking in foreign accents. They stayed at the Jiudun Temple in Huang Gonglou, causing great disorder. More than 50 able-bodied men in the village armed themselves and drove the disaster victims out of the area.

Recent Situation in Guangdong and Guangxi (IV) 85

— By Our Reporter Xiao'an

The Formation of the Fourth Route Army

The Guangdong army was repeatedly expanded during the Chen Jitang era, eventually consisting of five armies, each with three divisions, for a total of fifteen divisions. The troop strength was approximately 100,000, and the monthly military expenditure was more than 6 million yuan. After Yu Hanmou took over as the commander-in-chief of the Fourth Route Army, he was ordered to reduce the fifteen divisions to ten divisions, numbered from the First to the Tenth Division. When Chairman Chiang Kai-shek arrived in Guangdong, he reorganized the Guangdong army and brought the Guangdong army's flags and Central Army's flags into sequential order. In particular, he eliminated the local nature of the designations to show unity. Therefore, the designation of the First Division of the Guangdong Army was changed to the 151st Division of the Central Army, and the designation of the Second Division of the Guangdong Army was changed to the 152nd Division of the Central Army, and so on up to the 160th Division. The division commanders were initially not changed, namely Mo Xide as the commander of the 151st Division, Ye Zhao as the commander of the 152nd Division, Zhang Ruigui as the commander of the 153rd Division, Wu Jianxiong as the commander of the 154th Division, Li Hanhun as the commander of the 155th Division, Deng Longguang as the commander of the 156th Division, Huang Zhiwen as the commander of the 157th Division, Zeng Youren as the commander of the 158th Division, Tan Sui as the commander of the 159th Division, and Chen Hanguang as the commander of the 160th Division. Later, Yu Hanmou made slight changes to the division commanders, namely Chen Zhang as the commander of the 152nd Division, while the original commander of the 152nd Division, Ye Zhao, was transferred to be the commander of the 160th Division. Huang Tao was also appointed as the commander of the 157th Division, while the original commanders Huang Zhiwen and Chen Hanguang were transferred to be councillors of the Fourth Route Army Headquarters. Although the Guangdong army was reduced in size by Yu Hanmou and reorganized by Chiang Kai-shek, the number of soldiers dismissed was not large. The troop strength of each division was more substantial than during the Chen Jitang era.

The Fourth Route Army Headquarters decided to divide the province into five military districts and appointed Huang Renhuan, Zhang Lian, Miao Peinan, Li Zhenqiu, and Huang Yanzhen as the commanders of the military districts. The organization of the five military districts was similar to the five pacification zones of the past. It was originally planned to establish them immediately, but Huang Renhuan and others organized a national inspection tour to travel to various provinces to observe military affairs. Therefore, the establishment of the military district headquarters will be delayed for three months. Currently, all pacification matters in the province are carried out by the division commanders under the instructions of Yu Hanmou.

The Fourth Route Army Headquarters was formed by expanding the former First Army Headquarters. Yu Hanmou was appointed as the commander-in-chief of the Fourth Route Army as the commander of the First Army, and Li Xu Huan was appointed as the chief secretary of the Fourth Route Army Headquarters as the secretary-general of the First Army. The position of chief of staff of the Fourth Route Army Headquarters should have been filled by Luo Zicai, the chief of staff of the First Army, but Yu Hanmou appointed Xu Jingtang as the chief of staff of the Fourth Route Army Headquarters. It is said that Yu and Xu had a close relationship. At the same time, Yu believed that Xu had good relations with the Guizhou authorities and Li Jishen. Xu also had a good reputation in the Guangdong military, and appointing him as the chief of staff of the Fourth Route Army Headquarters would make it easier to deal with various parties. However, Luo Zicai felt that he had a deep history with the First Army and was unable to be promoted to the position of chief of staff of the Fourth Route Army Headquarters, and he was very disappointed. He resolutely requested to resign. Later, in order to resolve the misunderstanding, Yu Hanmou changed Luo's position to commander of the training brigade. It can be seen that Yu put a lot of effort into this matter. In addition, Huang Zhiwen, the former commander of the 157th Division, and Chen Hanguang, the former commander of the 160th Division, had very close relationships with Chen Jitang. After Chen went into retirement, he ordered Huang and Chen to pledge their allegiance to the central government and introduced Xiang Hanping and Li Yangjing to the central government, requesting that they be appointed. The central government accepted them, appointing Li as the commander-in-chief of the bandit suppression in the Zhejiang-Fujian-Jiangxi border area and planning to lead Huang and Chen's divisions to Fujian. However, the four brigade commanders of the two divisions telegraphed their strong opposition, and Li did not take office. Huang and Chen were relieved of their positions as division commanders, and Yu Hanmou appointed Huang Tao and Ye Zhao as their successors. Huang and Ye had a very close relationship with Yu Hanmou. Therefore, the Guangdong army is very united after Yu Hanmou's repeated measures. In addition to assigning the ten divisions, the Fourth Route Army Headquarters also established an officers' training corps at the old military academy established by Chen Jitang in Yantang, near Guangzhou. The surplus officers from the reduced divisions were all sent to the corps for training, with their salaries paid. In the future, more officers from the divisions may be transferred to the corps for training, in order to give the officers a deeper education. It can be seen that Yu Hanmou is putting a lot of effort into the Fourth Route Army.

Sun Ke Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday Morning: Discusses Tense Situation in Chahar and Suiyuan; Meets Huang Renhuan, Zhang Da, Gong Yanzhen; Awaits Ship to Guangdong to Attend Sun Yat-sen's State Funeral 86

According to Xin Sheng News Agency, Sun Ke, President of the Legislative Yuan, left Beijing by the 11:00 PM express train the night before and arrived at Zhenru Station at 6:50 AM yesterday morning. He returned to his private residence on Columbia Road to rest. Afterwards, he went out briefly. Upon returning to his residence, Huang Renhuan, Zhang Da, and Huang Yanzhen, three military district commanders of the Guangdong Fourth Route Army Domestic Military Inspection Group, accompanied by Wang Zhinan, secretary of the Songhu Garrison Command, visited him around 10:00 AM and had discussions. Situation in Chahar and Suiyuan

The reporter first inquired about the Sino-Japanese diplomatic issues. Mr. Sun stated that the diplomatic authorities would handle it appropriately, and he did not know the details. Regarding the situation in the north, Mr. Sun said that in eastern Suiyuan and northern Chahar, a certain party had recently instigated puppet troops to invade, creating a tense situation. Chairman of Suiyuan Province, Fu Zuoyi, and Chairman of Chahar Province, Liu Ruming, had already been ordered to dispatch troops to intercept them.

Attitude of Various Countries

Mr. Sun further answered the reporter's question about the attitude of European and American countries towards the current Sino-Japanese situation, stating that there was no clear indication. Europe itself has many disputes. Belgium's declaration of neutrality is intended to warn Germany and Italy, and also implies that it cannot assist France. Currently, China's situation requires self-determination. Regarding the British loan to China, it is not a cash loan but a purchase on credit.

Awaiting Ship South

Mr. Sun was nominated as the Central Representative for the state funeral of the late Chairman Hu of the Central Standing Committee. It is said that he is here awaiting a ship and will be heading south soon. However, it has not yet been decided whether he will travel with Mr. Wang Liangchou on the 20th, or whether President Ju (Zheng), President Xu (Chongzhi), and Mr. Chen Lifu will accompany him. Yarn Sales Increase Sharply; Factories Operate at Full Capacity; Coarse and Fine Yarn Are Simultaneously Cleared 91

According to the Huadong News Agency, yarn sales this year have broken the record of the past five years. Sales have increased sharply, and the previous phenomenon of "expensive cotton, cheap yarn" has disappeared. All factories are now operating at full capacity, rushing to ship goods day and night. Coarse and fine yarn, from 8-count, 16-count, 20-count, 24-count, and 32-count and so on, are all being cleared simultaneously. As of yesterday, the transaction volume of yarn reached over 1.1 million bales, and the transaction volume of cotton reached over 2.6 million dan. The Dasheng No. 2 Yarn Factory, which has been closed for a long time, will be taken over by the China Communications and Second Banks, and merged with the Nantong No. 1 Factory to expand its business.

Following the Postponement of the National Assembly, Should Group Re-elections Be Held? Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Submits a Request for Interpretation Yesterday 92

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce submitted a request to the Municipal Party Headquarters and the Bureau of Social Affairs yesterday, seeking an interpretation as to whether re-elections of people's organizations should be held following the postponement of the National Assembly. The original request stated: "Regarding the matter of submitting a request, the Silk and Satin Trade Association stated in a letter dated the 15th of this month that the members' general meeting of the trade association is held once a year, and half of the executive and supervisory committee members are re-elected every two years, which has been complied with in the past. Now, with the arrival of the seventh members' general meeting and the re-election of committee members, it was originally intended to be held simultaneously in September of this year, but it was postponed due to the handling of national elections. There is no clear provision on whether the trade association should convene a members' general meeting to re-elect committee members. We are writing to inquire, hoping that your esteemed association will provide detailed instructions so that we can follow them accordingly." The matter was received on August 26th of this year with your esteemed association's Executive Document No. 2481, citing Public Letter No. 3817 from the Central Department of Civil Training, which stated, "In order to strictly ensure the election of National Assembly representatives, after the promulgation of the National Assembly Election Law and before the opening of the National Assembly, all people's organizations in various places, except those undergoing reorganization or with special circumstances and approved by the local senior party headquarters after submitting a report to this department, shall suspend re-elections." Therefore, the holding of re-elections by the association should be postponed until after the opening of the National Assembly in accordance with the aforementioned instructions. However, there are still points that need to be researched, which are presented to your esteemed association separately: (1) The re-election of the association is only for the re-election of executive and supervisory committee members, while companies and firms in the same industry can join the association at any time in accordance with Article 7 of the Association Law. It is not related to the re-election process. According to normal practice, new members should only be suspended from joining the association one month before the re-election, and there are no restrictions at other times. In other words, the intention of postponing the re-election is to restrict the frequent changes of officials during the national election period, and its scope does not include refusing to accept new members. Now, the candidates for the National Assembly representatives to be elected by vocational groups have been nominated separately by the officials of each association, and the task of national elections has come to an end. From now on, the election of National Assembly representatives is the responsibility of the members of each association in accordance with Article 24 of the National Assembly Election Law. Therefore, it seems unnecessary in practice to restrict the re-election of association members until the opening of the National Assembly. (2) The term of office of association officials is four years, with half of them being re-elected every two years, and the standing committee members have a term of two years and can be re-elected once. If the association's re-election is postponed from May 14th of this year, the date of promulgation of the National Assembly Representatives Election Law, to the date of the opening of the National Assembly, the legally mandated term of office not exceeding four years will be broken, and the two-year term of office of the supervisory committee members who can be re-elected once will be extended to three years. If they are re-elected, how will the term of office be calculated? All these obstacles should be documented and submitted to your esteemed association for review, hoping that you will provide instructions for compliance, which will be for the public convenience."

Kong Xiangxi, Suffering from Overwork, Hospitalized Yesterday; High Blood Pressure and Poor Heart Function; Requires Three Weeks of Rest and Must Refuse Visitors 94

According to the Xin Sheng News Agency, Kong Xiangxi, Vice President of the Executive Yuan and Minister of Finance, was hospitalized at the Shanghai Sanitarium & Hospital on Rue Coulmiers at 9:00 AM yesterday due to overwork.
